degraded writes warn via header\\n- Kill 2 of 3 nodes (RF=2) — shard loss; 503 or partial per policy\\n- Kill 1 of 2 Miroir replicas — zero client-visible downtime\\n- `tc netem delay 500ms` on one node — search slows, no errors\\n- Restart a killed node — Miroir detects within health interval\\n- Kill a node mid-rebalance — pause + resume;
